import { Root, API, APIInfo, APIExample, Property } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/api'
import { Tabs, Tab } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/tabs'
import { Accordion, Accordions } from 'fumadocs-ui/components/accordion';

<Root>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.aggregated.get"}>

## aggregated-schema-get

Gets the aggregated schema.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"custom_schema_fragment_ids"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of custom schema fragment DONs which are to be aggregated.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

The leaf type. Used for inferring the default stage diagram and
tenant fragment ID.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"stock_schema_fragment_id"} type={"string"}>

The stock schema fragment which is to be aggregated.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.aggregated.get"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "schema": {}
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export interface AggregatedSchemaGetResponse {
  schema: AggregatedSchema;
}
/**
 * List of custom fields from multiple source fragments.
 */
export interface AggregatedSchema {}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<Tab value={"400"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "detail": "string",
  "message": "string",
  "type": "artifact_already_attached_to_a_parent",
  "existing_parent": "string",
  "is_same": true
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

```ts
export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */

  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorUnauthorizedUnauthenticated {}

```

</Accordion>

```ts
   * Error detail information.

   * The message associated with the error.
   */
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.aggregated.get"}>

## aggregated-schema-get-post

Gets the aggregated schema.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"custom_schema_fragment_ids"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of custom schema fragment DONs which are to be aggregated.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

The leaf type. Used for inferring the default stage diagram and
tenant fragment ID.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"per_object_schema"} type={"array of object"}>

Per object schema, if associated with the leaf type.

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Object Type"}>



</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"stock_schema_fragment_id"} type={"string"}>

The stock schema fragment which is to be aggregated.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.aggregated.get" \
  -d '{
  "custom_schema_fragment_ids": [
    "string"
  ],
  "leaf_type": "string",
  "per_object_schema": [
    {}
  ],
  "stock_schema_fragment_id": "string"
}'
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "schema": {}
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export interface AggregatedSchemaGetResponse {
  schema: AggregatedSchema;
}
/**
 * List of custom fields from multiple source fragments.
 */
export interface AggregatedSchema {}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

```json title="Example Response"
  "detail": "string",
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */

  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */

}

  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.custom.get"}>

## custom-schema-fragments-get

Gets a custom schema fragment.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom schema fragment.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.custom.get"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "fragment": {
    "type": "app_fragment",
    "created_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "display_id": "string",
    "id": "string",
    "modified_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "conditions": [
      {}
    ],
    "deprecated": true,
    "description": "string",
    "fields": [
      {
        "field_type": "array",
        "description": "string",
        "is_filterable": true,
        "is_immutable": true,
        "is_pii": true,
        "is_required": true,
        "mfz": {},
        "name": "string",
        "oasis": {},
        "origin": "string",
        "ui": {
          "create_view": {
            "is_hidden": true
          },
          "detail_view": {
            "is_hidden": true
          },
          "display_name": "string",
          "filter_view": {
            "is_hidden": true
          },
          "group_name": "string",
          "is_active_in_detail_view": true,
          "is_bulk_action_enabled": true,
          "is_groupable": true,
          "is_hidden": true,
          "is_hidden_during_create": true,
          "is_read_only": true,
          "is_shown_in_summary": true,
          "is_sortable": true,
          "list_view": {
            "is_hidden": true
          },
          "placeholder": "string",
          "summary_view": {
            "is_hidden": true
          },
          "tooltip": "string"
        },
        "default_value": true
      }
    ],
    "fragment_type": "app",
    "leaf_type": "string",
    "new_fragment_ref": {
      "type": "app_fragment",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string"
    },
    "old_fragment_ref": {
      "type": "app_fragment",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string"
    },
    "app": "string"
  }
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomSchemaFragment = AppFragment | CustomTypeFragment | TenantFragment;
export type AppFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  /**
   * App this fragment applies to.
   */
  app?: string;
};
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBase = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * The conditions associated with the fields.
   */
  conditions?: CustomSchemaFragmentCondition[];
  /**
   * Indicates if the fragment has been deprecated. Modifications to
   * this field are done in-place and don't result in creation of a new
   * fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  deprecated?: boolean;
  /**
   * Description of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this custom schema fragment.
   */
  fields?: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Type of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  fragment_type?: "app" | "custom_type" | "tenant";
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};

export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
/**
 * The condition associated with a field.
 */
export interface CustomSchemaFragmentCondition {}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * Filter view UI hint overrides.

   */

 */
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}
```

</APIExample>

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.custom.get"}>

## custom-schema-fragments-get-post

Gets a custom schema fragment.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom schema fragment.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.custom.get" \
  -d '{
  "id": "string"
}'
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomSchemaFragment = AppFragment | CustomTypeFragment | TenantFragment;
export type AppFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  /**
   * App this fragment applies to.
   */
  app?: string;
};
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBase = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * The conditions associated with the fields.
   */
  conditions?: CustomSchemaFragmentCondition[];
  /**
   * Indicates if the fragment has been deprecated. Modifications to
   * this field are done in-place and don't result in creation of a new
   * fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  deprecated?: boolean;
  /**
   * Description of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this custom schema fragment.
   */
  fields?: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Type of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  fragment_type?: "app" | "custom_type" | "tenant";
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};

  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};

   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;
};

   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};

export type CustomSchemaFragmentSummary = AppFragmentSummary | CustomTypeFragmentSummary | TenantFragmentSummary;
export type AppFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  stage_diagram?: StageDiagramSummary;
  /**
   * The string used to populate the subtype in the leaf type.
   *
   */
  subtype?: string;
  /**
   * Display name of the subtype. Modifications to this field are done
   * in-place and don't result in creation of a new fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  subtype_display_name?: string;
};
export type StageDiagramSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase;

export interface CustomSchemaFragmentsGetResponse {
  fragment: CustomSchemaFragment;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
/**
 * The condition associated with a field.
 */
export interface CustomSchemaFragmentCondition {}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */

/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */

  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;

   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;

 * Filter view UI hint overrides.

  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
   */

   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI list view.

 * Summary view UI hint overrides.

  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI summary view.
   */

 */
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}
```

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.custom.list"}>

## custom-schema-fragments-list

Lists custom schema fragments.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"app"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of app names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from. If not provided, then iteration
starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"deprecated"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether only deprecated fragments should be filtered.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of leaf types.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"mode"} type={"string"}>

The iteration mode to use, otherwise if not set, then "after" is
used.


<span>Value in:  `"after" | "before"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"prune"} type={"array of string"}>

List of fields which are not required in the payload and can be
pruned away.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"subtype"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of subtypes.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"types"} type={"array of string"}>

Filters for custom schema fragment of the provided types.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.custom.list"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "next_cursor": "string",
  "prev_cursor": "string",
  "result": [
    {
      "type": "app_fragment",
      "created_by": {
        "type": "dev_user",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string",
        "display_picture": {
          "display_id": "string",
          "id": "string"
        },
        "email": "string",
        "full_name": "string",
        "state": "active"
      },
      "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "modified_by": {
        "type": "dev_user",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string",
        "display_picture": {
          "display_id": "string",
          "id": "string"
        },
        "email": "string",
        "full_name": "string",
        "state": "active"
      },
      "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
      "conditions": [
        {}
      ],
      "deprecated": true,
      "description": "string",
      "fields": [
        {
          "field_type": "array",
          "description": "string",
          "is_filterable": true,
          "is_immutable": true,
          "is_pii": true,
          "is_required": true,
          "mfz": {},
          "name": "string",
          "oasis": {},
          "origin": "string",
          "ui": {
            "create_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "detail_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "display_name": "string",
            "filter_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "group_name": "string",
            "is_active_in_detail_view": true,
            "is_bulk_action_enabled": true,
            "is_groupable": true,
            "is_hidden": true,
            "is_hidden_during_create": true,
            "is_read_only": true,
            "is_shown_in_summary": true,
            "is_sortable": true,
            "list_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "placeholder": "string",
            "summary_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "tooltip": "string"
          },
          "default_value": true
        }
      ],
      "fragment_type": "app",
      "leaf_type": "string",
      "new_fragment_ref": {
        "type": "app_fragment",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "old_fragment_ref": {
        "type": "app_fragment",
        "display_id": "string",
```

```ts
export type CustomSchemaFragment = AppFragment | CustomTypeFragment | TenantFragment;
export type AppFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  /**
   * App this fragment applies to.
   */
  app?: string;
};
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBase = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * The conditions associated with the fields.
   */
  conditions?: CustomSchemaFragmentCondition[];
  /**
   * Indicates if the fragment has been deprecated. Modifications to
   * this field are done in-place and don't result in creation of a new
   * fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  deprecated?: boolean;
  /**
   * Description of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this custom schema fragment.
   */
  fields?: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Type of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  fragment_type?: "app" | "custom_type" | "tenant";
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;
};
export type SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType =
  | SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumListFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean[];
};
export type SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number[];
};

   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];

   * Default value.

  lt?: number;

   * The maximum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  lte?: number;
};

   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};

export type CustomSchemaFragmentSummary = AppFragmentSummary | CustomTypeFragmentSummary | TenantFragmentSummary;
export type AppFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  stage_diagram?: StageDiagramSummary;
  /**
   * The string used to populate the subtype in the leaf type.
   *
   */
  subtype?: string;
  /**
   * Display name of the subtype. Modifications to this field are done
   * in-place and don't result in creation of a new fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  subtype_display_name?: string;
};
export type StageDiagramSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase;

export interface CustomSchemaFragmentsListResponse {
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate subsequent results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no later elements exist.
   *
   */
  next_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate preceding results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no prior elements exist.
   *
   */
  prev_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The custom schema fragments.
   */
  result: CustomSchemaFragment[];
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
/**
 * The condition associated with a field.
 */
export interface CustomSchemaFragmentCondition {}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * Filter view UI hint overrides.

   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorServiceUnavailable = ErrorBase & ErrorServiceUnavailableServiceUnavailable;

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorServiceUnavailableServiceUnavailable {}
```

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.custom.list"}>

## custom-schema-fragments-list-post

Lists custom schema fragments.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"app"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of app names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from. If not provided, then
iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"deprecated"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether only deprecated fragments should be filtered.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of leaf types.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"mode"} type={"string"}>

The iteration mode to use. If "after", then entries after the provided
cursor will be returned, or if no cursor is provided, then from the
beginning. If "before", then entries before the provided cursor will be
returned, or if no cursor is provided, then from the end. Entries will
always be returned in the specified sort-by order.


<span>Value in:  `"after" | "before"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"prune"} type={"array of string"}>

List of fields which are not required in the payload and can be
pruned away.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"subtype"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of subtypes.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"types"} type={"array of string"}>

Filters for custom schema fragment of the provided types.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.custom.list" \
  -d '{
  "app": [
    "string"
  ],
  "cursor": "string",
  "deprecated": true,
  "leaf_type": [
    "string"
  ],
  "limit": 0,
  "mode": "after",
  "prune": [
    "fields"
  ],
  "sort_by": [
    "string"
  ],
  "subtype": [
    "string"
  ],
  "types": [
    "app_fragment"
  ]
}'
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

```ts
export type CustomSchemaFragment = AppFragment | CustomTypeFragment | TenantFragment;
export type AppFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  /**
   * App this fragment applies to.
   */
  app?: string;
};
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBase = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * The conditions associated with the fields.
   */
  conditions?: CustomSchemaFragmentCondition[];
  /**
   * Indicates if the fragment has been deprecated. Modifications to
   * this field are done in-place and don't result in creation of a new
   * fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  deprecated?: boolean;
  /**
   * Description of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this custom schema fragment.
   */
  fields?: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Type of the custom schema fragment.
   */
  fragment_type?: "app" | "custom_type" | "tenant";
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: CustomSchemaFragmentSummary;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;
};
export type SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType =
  | SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumListFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean[];
};
export type SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number[];
};
export type SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * Object ID types. Required when field type is ID.
   */
  id_type?: string[];
};
export type SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number[];
  /**
   * The minimum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  gt?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  gte?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  lt?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  lte?: number;
};
export type SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * The contained substring.
   */
  contains?: string;
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * The exact string length.
   */
  eq_len?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum string length.
   */
  max_len?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum string length.
   */
  min_len?: number;
  /**
   * The string pattern (regular expression).
   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};
export type SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * The contained substring.
   */
  contains?: string;
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * The exact string length.
   */
  eq_len?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum string length.
   */
  max_len?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum string length.
   */
  min_len?: number;
  /**
   * The string pattern (regular expression).
   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};
export type SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {

   * Default value.

  default_value?: string[];
};

  eq_len?: number;

   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;

export type SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentSummary = AppFragmentSummary | CustomTypeFragmentSummary | TenantFragmentSummary;
export type AppFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomTypeFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase & {
  stage_diagram?: StageDiagramSummary;
  /**
   * The string used to populate the subtype in the leaf type.
   *
   */
  subtype?: string;
  /**
   * Display name of the subtype. Modifications to this field are done
   * in-place and don't result in creation of a new fragment in chain.
   *
   */
  subtype_display_name?: string;
};
export type StageDiagramSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragment = CustomSchemaFragmentBase;

export interface CustomSchemaFragmentsListResponse {
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate subsequent results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no later elements exist.
   *
   */
  next_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate preceding results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no prior elements exist.
   *
   */
  prev_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The custom schema fragments.
   */
  result: CustomSchemaFragment[];
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
/**
 * The condition associated with a field.
 */
export interface CustomSchemaFragmentCondition {}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Filter view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * List view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI list view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Summary view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * A unified enum value.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUenumValue {}
```

```json title="Example Response"
  "message": "string",
  "type": "artifact_already_attached_to_a_parent",
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.custom.set"}>

## custom-schema-fragments-set

Creates or updates a custom schema fragment.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"conditions"} type={"array of object"}>

List of conditions for this fragment.

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Object Type"}>



</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"deleted_fields"} type={"array of string"}>

List of field names which are being dropped.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"deprecated"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether this fragment has been deprecated.

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"description"} type={"string"}>

The description of the custom schema fragment.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"fields"} type={"array of object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object & object | object"}>

List of all fields in this fragment.

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Object Type"}>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"field_type"} type={"string"}>



<span>Value in:  `"array" | "bool" | "composite" | "date" | "double" | "enum" | "id" | "int" | "rich_text" | "text" | "timestamp" | "tokens" | "uenum" | "unknown"`</span>

</Property>

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"is_custom_leaf_type"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether the leaf type corresponds to a custom object

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

The leaf type this fragment applies to.

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"type"} type={"string"}>



<span>Value in:  `"app_fragment" | "custom_type_fragment" | "tenant_fragment"`</span>

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `201` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.custom.set" \
  -d '{
  "conditions": [
    {}
  ],
  "deleted_fields": [
    "string"
  ],
  "deprecated": true,
  "description": "string",
  "fields": [
    {
      "field_type": "array",
      "description": "string",
      "is_filterable": true,
      "is_immutable": true,
      "is_pii": true,
      "is_required": true,
      "mfz": {},
      "name": "string",
      "oasis": {},
      "origin": "string",
      "ui": {
        "create_view": {
          "is_hidden": true
        },
        "detail_view": {
          "is_hidden": true
        },
        "display_name": "string",
        "filter_view": {
          "is_hidden": true
        },
        "group_name": "string",
        "is_active_in_detail_view": true,
        "is_bulk_action_enabled": true,
        "is_groupable": true,
        "is_hidden": true,
        "is_hidden_during_create": true,
        "is_read_only": true,
        "is_shown_in_summary": true,
        "is_sortable": true,
        "list_view": {
          "is_hidden": true
        },
        "placeholder": "string",
        "summary_view": {
          "is_hidden": true
        },
        "tooltip": "string"
      },
      "default_value": true
    }
  ],
  "is_custom_leaf_type": true,
  "leaf_type": "string",
  "type": "app_fragment",
  "app": "string"
}'
```
