```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
```
```ts
}

```

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.stock.get"}>

## stock-schema-fragments-get

Gets a stock schema fragment.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the stock schema fragment.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

The leaf type this fragment applies to.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>



<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type StockSchemaFragment = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * Description of the schema.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this schema.
   */
  fields: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the schema.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;
};
export type SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType =
  | SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumListFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean[];
};
export type SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number[];
};
export type SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * Object ID types. Required when field type is ID.
   */
  id_type?: string[];
};
export type SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number[];
  /**
   * The minimum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  gt?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  gte?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  lt?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  lte?: number;
};
export type SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * The contained substring.
   */
  contains?: string;
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * The exact string length.
   */
  eq_len?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum string length.
   */
  max_len?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum string length.
   */
  min_len?: number;
  /**
   * The string pattern (regular expression).
   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};
export type SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * The contained substring.
   */
  contains?: string;
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
  /**
   * The exact string length.
   */
  eq_len?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum string length.
   */
  max_len?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum string length.
   */
  min_len?: number;
  /**
   * The string pattern (regular expression).
   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};
export type SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};
export type SchemaTokensListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * The contained substring.

  contains?: string;
  /**
   * Default value.

  default_value?: string[];

   * The exact string length.

   * The minimum string length.

  pattern?: string;

   * The string prefix.

  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.

  suffix?: string;

   * Allowed values for the field.
   */

  /**
   * Default value.
   */

   * Default value.
   */

   * Object ID types. Required when field type is ID.
   */
  id_type?: string[];
};

   * Default value.
   */

   * The minimum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  gt?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  gte?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (exclusive).
   */
  lt?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum value for the integer (inclusive).
   */
  lte?: number;
};

  /**
   * The exact string length.

  eq_len?: number;
  /**
   * The maximum string length.
   */
  max_len?: number;
  /**
   * The minimum string length.
   */
  min_len?: number;
  /**
   * The string pattern (regular expression).
   */
  pattern?: string;
  /**
   * The string prefix.
   */
  prefix?: string;
  /**
   * The string suffix.
   */
  suffix?: string;
};

  | AccountSummary
  | AppFragmentSummary
  | CapabilitySummary
  | ConversationSummary

  | EngagementSummary

export type CapabilitySummary = PartBaseSummary;

  /**
   * Name of the part.
   */
  name: string;
};

  /**
   * Title of the conversation object.
   */

};
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;

export type FeatureSummary = PartBaseSummary;

  /**
   * Priority of the work based upon impact and criticality.
   */

};

  /**
   * The users that own the work.
   */

  stage?: LegacyStageSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the work object.
   */
  title: string;
};
export type MeetingSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type OpportunitySummary = WorkBaseSummary;
export type ProductSummary = PartBaseSummary;

   * The name of the tag, which denotes the logical concept by which all
   * tagged objects will be associated. The name is guaranteed to be
   * unique.
   *
   */
  name: string;
};
export type TaskSummary = WorkBaseSummary;

};

  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Filter view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * List view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI list view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * Summary view UI hint overrides.
 */

  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * A unified enum value.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUenumValue {}

 * Describes the current stage of a work item.
 */

  /**
   * Current stage name of the work item.
   */
  name: string;
}
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}
```

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.stock.get"}>

## stock-schema-fragments-get-post

Gets a stock schema fragment.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the stock schema fragment.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

The leaf type this fragment applies to.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.stock.get" \
  -d '{
  "id": "string",
  "leaf_type": "string"
}'
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type StockSchemaFragment = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * Description of the schema.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this schema.
   */
  fields: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the schema.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */
export type SchemaFieldDescriptor =
  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType
  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};
export type SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: number;
};
export type SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};
export type SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType =
  | SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIdListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensListFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumListFieldDescriptor;
export type SchemaBoolListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean[];
};
export type SchemaCompositeListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};
export type SchemaDateListFieldDescriptor = SchemaFieldDescriptorBase & {
  /**
   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string[];
};

   * Default value.

};

   * Default value.

};

   * Default value.

   * Object ID types. Required when field type is ID.

   * Default value.

   * The minimum value for the integer (exclusive).

  lte?: number;

export type AtomSummary =
  | AccountSummary
  | AppFragmentSummary
  | CapabilitySummary
  | ConversationSummary
  | CustomTypeFragmentSummary
  | DevUserSummary
  | EngagementSummary
  | EnhancementSummary
  | FeatureSummary
  | IssueSummary
  | MeetingSummary
  | OpportunitySummary
  | ProductSummary
  | RevOrgSummary
  | RevUserSummary
  | ServiceAccountSummary
  | SysUserSummary
  | TagSummary
  | TaskSummary
  | TenantFragmentSummary
  | TicketSummary
  | TimelineCommentSummary
  | WebhookSummary;
export type AppFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type CapabilitySummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type PartBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the part.
   */
  name: string;
};
export type ConversationSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Title of the conversation object.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type EngagementSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type EnhancementSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type FeatureSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type IssueSummary = WorkBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Priority of the work based upon impact and criticality.
   */
  priority?: "p0" | "p1" | "p2" | "p3";
};
export type WorkBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The users that own the work.
   */
  owned_by: UserSummary[];
  stage?: LegacyStageSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the work object.
   */
  title: string;
};
export type MeetingSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type OpportunitySummary = WorkBaseSummary;
export type ProductSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type TagSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The name of the tag, which denotes the logical concept by which all
   * tagged objects will be associated. The name is guaranteed to be
   * unique.
   *
   */
  name: string;
};
export type TaskSummary = WorkBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type TicketSummary = WorkBaseSummary & {
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
  /**
   * Severity of the ticket.
   */
  severity?: "blocker" | "high" | "low" | "medium";
};
export type TimelineCommentSummary = TimelineEntryBaseSummary;
export type TimelineEntryBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type WebhookSummary = AtomBaseSummary;

export interface StockSchemaFragmentsGetResponse {
  fragment: StockSchemaFragment;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Filter view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * List view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI list view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Summary view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * A unified enum value.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUenumValue {}
/**
 * Describes the current stage of a work item.
 */
export interface LegacyStageSummary {
  /**
   * Current stage name of the work item.
   */
  name: string;
}
```

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.stock.list"}>

## stock-schema-fragments-list

Lists stock schema fragments.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from. If not provided, then iteration
starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"filter_preset"} type={"string"}>

Filter preset to specify whether to filter only customization enabled
leaf types.


<span>Value in:  `"customizable_types_preset" | "no_preset"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of leaf types.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"mode"} type={"string"}>

The iteration mode to use, otherwise if not set, then "after" is
used.


<span>Value in:  `"after" | "before"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"prune"} type={"array of string"}>

List of fields which are not required in the payload and can be
pruned away.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.stock.list"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

```json title="Example Response"
            "is_active_in_detail_view": true,
            "is_bulk_action_enabled": true,
            "is_groupable": true,
            "is_hidden": true,
            "is_hidden_during_create": true,
            "is_read_only": true,
            "is_shown_in_summary": true,
            "is_sortable": true,
            "list_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "placeholder": "string",
            "summary_view": {
              "is_hidden": true
            },
            "tooltip": "string"
          },
          "default_value": true
        }
      ],
      "leaf_type": "string",
      "new_fragment_ref": {
        "type": "account",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string"
      },
      "old_fragment_ref": {
        "type": "account",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string"
      },
      "title": "string"
    }
  ]
}
```

```ts
export type StockSchemaFragment = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * Description of the schema.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this schema.
   */
  fields: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the schema.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;

   * Name of the Organization.

  display_name?: string;

  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor

  | SchemaIdFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor

  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;

   * Default value.
   */

};

   * Composite type. Required when field type is composite.
   */
  composite_type?: string;
};

   * Default value.

  name: string;

   * Description of the field.
   */

   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *

   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */

   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *

   * Name of the field.

   * Type this field is from.

   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

```ts
export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
```

```ts
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorServiceUnavailableServiceUnavailable {}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

</Tabs>

</APIExample>

</API>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/schemas.stock.list"}>

## stock-schema-fragments-list-post

Lists stock schema fragments.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from. If not provided, then
iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"filter_preset"} type={"string"}>



<span>Value in:  `"customizable_types_preset" | "no_preset"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_type"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of leaf types.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"mode"} type={"string"}>

The iteration mode to use. If "after", then entries after the provided
cursor will be returned, or if no cursor is provided, then from the
beginning. If "before", then entries before the provided cursor will be
returned, or if no cursor is provided, then from the end. Entries will
always be returned in the specified sort-by order.


<span>Value in:  `"after" | "before"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"prune"} type={"array of string"}>

List of fields which are not required in the payload and can be
pruned away.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.stock.list" \
  -d '{
  "cursor": "string",
  "filter_preset": "customizable_types_preset",
  "leaf_type": [
    "string"
  ],
  "limit": 0,
  "mode": "after",
  "prune": [
    "composite_schemas"
  ],
  "sort_by": [
    "string"
  ]
}'
```

```ts
export type StockSchemaFragment = AtomBase & {
  /**
   * Description of the schema.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * List of all fields in this schema.
   */
  fields: SchemaFieldDescriptor[];
  /**
   * Leaf type this fragment applies to.
   */
  leaf_type?: string;
  new_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  old_fragment_ref?: AtomSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the schema.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
/**
 * Set of field attributes.
 */

  | SchemaBoolFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaCompositeFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDateFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaDoubleFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaEnumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaFieldDescriptorArrayType

  | SchemaIntFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaRichTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTextFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTimestampFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaTokensFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUenumFieldDescriptor
  | SchemaUnknownFieldDescriptor;

   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: boolean;
};

   */
  composite_type?: string;

   * Default value.
   */
  default_value?: string;
};

export type AtomSummary =
  | AccountSummary
  | AppFragmentSummary
  | CapabilitySummary
  | ConversationSummary
  | CustomTypeFragmentSummary
  | DevUserSummary
  | EngagementSummary
  | EnhancementSummary
  | FeatureSummary
  | IssueSummary
  | MeetingSummary
  | OpportunitySummary
  | ProductSummary
  | RevOrgSummary
  | RevUserSummary
  | ServiceAccountSummary
  | SysUserSummary
  | TagSummary
  | TaskSummary
  | TenantFragmentSummary
  | TicketSummary
  | TimelineCommentSummary
  | WebhookSummary;
export type AppFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type CapabilitySummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type PartBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the part.
   */
  name: string;
};
export type ConversationSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Title of the conversation object.
   */
  title?: string;
};
export type CustomTypeFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type EngagementSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type EnhancementSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type FeatureSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type IssueSummary = WorkBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Priority of the work based upon impact and criticality.
   */
  priority?: "p0" | "p1" | "p2" | "p3";
};
export type WorkBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The users that own the work.
   */
  owned_by: UserSummary[];
  stage?: LegacyStageSummary;
  /**
   * Title of the work object.
   */
  title: string;
};
export type MeetingSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type OpportunitySummary = WorkBaseSummary;
export type ProductSummary = PartBaseSummary;
export type TagSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The name of the tag, which denotes the logical concept by which all
   * tagged objects will be associated. The name is guaranteed to be
   * unique.
   *
   */
  name: string;
};
export type TaskSummary = WorkBaseSummary;
export type TenantFragmentSummary = CustomSchemaFragmentBaseSummary;
export type TicketSummary = WorkBaseSummary & {
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
  /**
   * Severity of the ticket.
   */
  severity?: "blocker" | "high" | "low" | "medium";
};
export type TimelineCommentSummary = TimelineEntryBaseSummary;
export type TimelineEntryBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type WebhookSummary = AtomBaseSummary;

export interface StockSchemaFragmentsListResponse {
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate subsequent results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no later elements exist.
   *
   */
  next_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The cursor used to iterate preceding results in accordance to the
   * sort order. If not set, then no prior elements exist.
   *
   */
  prev_cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The stock schema fragments.
   */
  result: StockSchemaFragment[];
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
export interface SchemaFieldDescriptorBase {
  /**
   * Description of the field.
   */
  description?: string;
  /**
   * Whether this field is filterable, groupable and sortable.
   *
   */
  is_filterable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is immutable or not.
   */
  is_immutable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field can hold Personally Identifiable Information
   * (PII).
   *
   */
  is_pii?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether this field is required or not.
   */
  is_required?: boolean;
  mfz?: SchemaFieldMfzMetadata;
  /**
   * Name of the field.
   */
  name: string;
  oasis?: SchemaFieldOasisMetadata;
  /**
   * Type this field is from.
   */
  origin?: string;
  ui?: SchemaFieldUiMetadata;
}
/**
 * The schema of MFZ specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldMfzMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of oasis specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldOasisMetadata {}
/**
 * The schema of ui specific fields.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUiMetadata {
  create_view?: SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata;
  detail_view?: SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * The display name of the field.
   */
  display_name?: string;
  filter_view?: SchemaFieldFilterViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * An optional group name for the field.
   */
  group_name?: string;
  /**
   * Whether the field is active in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_active_in_detail_view?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field supports bulk action.
   */
  is_bulk_action_enabled?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is groupable in the UI.
   */
  is_groupable?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI during creation.
   */
  is_hidden_during_create?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is read-only in the UI.
   */
  is_read_only?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is shown in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_shown_in_summary?: boolean;
  /**
   * Whether the field is sortable in the UI.
   */
  is_sortable?: boolean;
  list_view?: SchemaFieldListViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * A placeholder for the field.
   */
  placeholder?: string;
  summary_view?: SchemaFieldSummaryViewUiMetadata;
  /**
   * Tooltip for the field.
   */
  tooltip?: string;
}
/**
 * Create view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldCreateViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI create view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Detail view UI hint overrides.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldDetailViewUiMetadata {
  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI detail view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * Filter view UI hint overrides.
 */

   * Whether field is hidden in the UI filter view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}

 * List view UI hint overrides.
 */

  /**
   * Whether the field is hidden in the UI list view.
   */

}

 * Summary view UI hint overrides.
 */

  /**
   * Whether field is hidden in the UI summary view.
   */
  is_hidden?: boolean;
}
/**
 * A unified enum value.
 */
export interface SchemaFieldUenumValue {}
/**
 * Describes the current stage of a work item.
 */
export interface LegacyStageSummary {
  /**
   * Current stage name of the work item.
   */
  name: string;
}
```

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/schemas.subtypes.list"}>

## subtypes-list

Lists subtypes.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={true} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

Leaf type for which subtypes are required.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_types"} type={"array of string"}>

List of leaf types for which subtypes are required.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.subtypes.list"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "subtypes": [
    {
      "display_name": "string",
      "fragment_id": "string",
      "leaf_type": "string",
      "value": "string"
    }
  ]
}
```

```ts
   * Display name of the subtype.
   */

  /**
   * Leaf type for the subtype.
   */

  /**
   * Value of the subtype.
   */
```

```ts
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField

   * The message associated with the error.
```

## subtypes-list-post

Lists subtypes.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={true} name={"leaf_type"} type={"string"}>

Leaf type for which subtypes are required.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"leaf_types"} type={"array of string"}>

List of leaf types for which subtypes are required.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/schemas.subtypes.list" \
  -d '{
  "leaf_type": "string",
  "leaf_types": [
    "string"
  ]
}'
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/stages.custom.create"}>

## custom-stages-create

Creates a custom stage.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"marketplace_ref"} type={"string"}>

A reference to the marketplace item from which this stage was
imported.


</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"string"}>

The name of the custom stage.

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"integer"}>

The ordinal of the custom stage used for ordering.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"state"} type={"string"}>

The state ID.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `201` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/stages.custom.create" \
  -d '{
  "marketplace_ref": "string",
  "name": "string",
  "ordinal": 0,
  "state": "string"
}'
```

<Tabs items={["201","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"201"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "custom_stage": {
    "created_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "display_id": "string",
    "id": "string",
    "modified_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z"
  }
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomStage = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStagesCreateResponse {
  custom_stage: CustomStage;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<Tab value={"400"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "detail": "string",
  "message": "string",
  "type": "artifact_already_attached_to_a_parent",
  "existing_parent": "string",
  "is_same": true
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

```json title="Example Response"

  "detail": "string",
  "message": "string",
  "type": "unauthenticated"
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/stages.custom.get"}>

## custom-stages-get

Gets a custom stage.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom stage to get.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/stages.custom.get"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "custom_stage": {
    "created_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "display_id": "string",
    "id": "string",
    "modified_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z"
  }
}
```

```ts
export type CustomStage = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStagesGetResponse {
  custom_stage: CustomStage;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}

  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}
```

## custom-stages-get-post

Gets a custom stage.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

```ts
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>
