<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/stages.custom.list"}>

## custom-stages-list

Lists custom stages.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided, then
iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of stage names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"array of integer"}>

The list of stage ordinals.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/stages.custom.list"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "cursor": "string",
  "result": [
    {
      "created_by": {
        "type": "dev_user",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string",
        "display_picture": {
          "display_id": "string",
          "id": "string"
        },
        "email": "string",
        "full_name": "string",
        "state": "active"
      },
      "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "modified_by": {
        "type": "dev_user",
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string",
        "display_name": "string",
        "display_picture": {
          "display_id": "string",
          "id": "string"
        },
        "email": "string",
        "full_name": "string",
        "state": "active"
      },
      "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z"
    }
  ]
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomStage = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStagesListResponse {
  /**
   * The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided,
   * then iteration starts from the beginning.
   *
   */
  cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The custom stages.
   */
  result: CustomStage[];
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

```ts
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
```

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/stages.custom.list"}>

## custom-stages-list-post

Lists custom stages.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided,
then iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of stage names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"array of integer"}>

The list of stage ordinals.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/stages.custom.list" \
  -d '{
  "cursor": "string",
  "limit": 0,
  "name": [
    "string"
  ],
  "ordinal": [
    0
  ],
  "sort_by": [
    "string"
  ]
}'
```

```ts
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<API>

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/stages.custom.update"}>

## custom-stages-update

Updates a custom stage.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom stage to update.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"string"}>

The updated name of the custom stage.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"integer"}>

The ordinal of the custom stage.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"state_id"} type={"string"}>

The state ID.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/stages.custom.update" \
  -d '{
  "id": "string",
  "name": "string",
  "ordinal": 0,
  "state_id": "string"
}'
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "custom_stage": {
    "created_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "display_id": "string",
    "id": "string",
    "modified_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z"
  }
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomStage = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStagesUpdateResponse {
  custom_stage: CustomStage;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}

  /**
   * The missing field's name.

  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */

  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;

   */
```

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/states.custom.create"}>

## custom-states-create

Creates a custom state.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"is_final"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether this is a final state.

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"string"}>

The name of the custom state.

</Property>

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"integer"}>

Ordinal of the custom state used to identify system states.


<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `201` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"

  -d '{
  "is_final": true,

  "ordinal": 0
}'
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/states.custom.get"}>

## custom-states-get

Gets a custom state.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom state to get.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/states.custom.get"
```

<Tabs items={["200","400","401","403","404","429","500","503"]}>

<Tab value={"200"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "custom_state": {
    "created_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "created_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z",
    "display_id": "string",
    "id": "string",
    "modified_by": {
      "type": "dev_user",
      "display_id": "string",
      "id": "string",
      "display_name": "string",
      "display_picture": {
        "display_id": "string",
        "id": "string"
      },
      "email": "string",
      "full_name": "string",
      "state": "active"
    },
    "modified_date": "2023-01-01T12:00:00.000Z"
  }
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomState = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStatesGetResponse {
  custom_state: CustomState;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<Tab value={"400"}>



```json title="Example Response"
{
  "detail": "string",
  "message": "string",
  "type": "artifact_already_attached_to_a_parent",
  "existing_parent": "string",
  "is_same": true
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

## custom-states-get-post

Gets a custom state.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom state to get.

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/states.custom.get" \
  -d '{
  "id": "string"
}'
```

<API>

<APIInfo method={"GET"} route={"/states.custom.list"}>

## custom-states-list

Lists custom states.

### Query Parameters

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided, then
iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"is_final"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether only final states should be filtered.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of state names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"array of integer"}>

The list of state ordinals.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X GET "https://api.devrev.ai/states.custom.list"
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomState = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStatesListResponse {
  /**
   * The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided,
   * then iteration starts from the beginning.
   *
   */
  cursor?: string;
  /**
   * The custom states.
   */
  result: CustomState[];
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

```json title="Example Response"
  "type": "artifact_already_attached_to_a_parent",
  "existing_parent": "string",
  "is_same": true
}
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

## custom-states-list-post

Lists custom states.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"cursor"} type={"string"}>

The cursor to resume iteration from, otherwise if not provided,
then iteration starts from the beginning.


</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"is_final"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether only final states should be filtered.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"limit"} type={"integer"}>

The maximum number of items.

<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of state names.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"array of integer"}>

The list of state ordinals.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"sort_by"} type={"array of string"}>

The list of fields to sort the items by and how to sort them.


</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

```bash title="curl"
    "string"
  ],
  "ordinal": [

    "string"
  ]
```

<APIInfo method={"POST"} route={"/states.custom.update"}>

## custom-states-update

Updates a custom state.

### Request Body (Optional)



<Property required={true} deprecated={false} name={"id"} type={"string"}>

The ID of the custom state to update.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"is_final"} type={"boolean"}>

Whether this is a final state.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"name"} type={"string"}>

The name of the custom state.

</Property>

<Property required={false} deprecated={false} name={"ordinal"} type={"integer"}>

Ordinal of the custom state used to identify system states.


<span>Format:  `"int32"`</span>

</Property>

| Status code | Description |
| ----------- | ----------- |
| `200` | Success. |
| `400` | 400 Bad Request. |
| `401` | 401 Unauthorized. |
| `403` | 403 Forbidden. |
| `404` | 404 Not Found. |
| `429` | 429 Too Many Requests. |
| `500` | 500 Internal Server Error. |
| `503` | 503 Service Unavailable. |

</APIInfo>

<APIExample>

```bash title="curl"
curl -X POST "https://api.devrev.ai/states.custom.update" \
  -d '{
  "id": "string",
  "is_final": true,
  "name": "string",
  "ordinal": 0
}'
```

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type CustomState = AtomBase;
export type UserSummary = DevUserSummary | RevUserSummary | ServiceAccountSummary | SysUserSummary;
export type DevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type UserBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * The user's display name. The name is non-unique and mutable.
   *
   */
  display_name?: string;
  display_picture?: ArtifactSummary;
  /**
   * Email address of the user.
   */
  email?: string;
  /**
   * Full name of the user.
   */
  full_name?: string;
  /**
   * State of the user.
   */
  state?: "active" | "deactivated" | "deleted" | "locked" | "shadow" | "unassigned";
};
export type ArtifactSummary = AtomBaseSummary;
export type RevUserSummary = UserBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * External ref is a mutable unique identifier for a user within the
   * Rev organization from your primary customer record. If none is
   * available, a good alternative is the email address/phone number
   * which could uniquely identify the user. If none is specified, a
   * system-generated identifier will be assigned to the user.
   *
   */
  external_ref?: string;
  rev_org?: OrgSummary;
};
export type OrgSummary = AccountSummary | RevOrgSummary;
export type AccountSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type OrgBaseSummary = AtomBaseSummary & {
  /**
   * Name of the Organization.
   */
  display_name?: string;
};
export type RevOrgSummary = OrgBaseSummary;
export type ServiceAccountSummary = UserBaseSummary;
export type SysUserSummary = UserBaseSummary;

export interface CustomStatesUpdateResponse {
  custom_state: CustomState;
}
export interface AtomBase {
  created_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was created.
   */
  created_date?: string;
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
  modified_by?: UserSummary;
  /**
   * Timestamp when the object was last modified.
   */
  modified_date?: string;
}
export interface AtomBaseSummary {
  /**
   * Human-readable object ID unique to the Dev organization.
   */
  display_id?: string;
  /**
   * Globally unique object ID.
   */
  id: string;
}

```

</Accordion>

</Accordions>

</Tab>

<Accordions>

<Accordion title={"Typescript Definition"}>

```ts
export type ErrorBadRequest = ErrorBase &
  (
    | ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent
    | ErrorBadRequestBadRequest
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue
    | ErrorBadRequestInvalidField
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency
    | ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField
    | ErrorBadRequestParseError
    | ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments
    | ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType
    | ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted
  );

export interface ErrorBase {
  /**
   * Error detail information.
   */
  detail?: string;
  /**
   * The message associated with the error.
   */
  message?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestArtifactAlreadyAttachedToAParent {
  /**
   * The existing parent attached to the artifact.
   */
  existing_parent: string;
  /**
   * Whether the existing parent is the same as the new parent.
   *
   */
  is_same: boolean;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestBadRequest {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidApiVersion {
  /**
   * The provided API version.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidEnumValue {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose enum value is invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestInvalidField {
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent fields.
   */
  dependencies?: ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency[];
  /**
   * The field on which the value depends.
   */
  dependent_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value which needs to be set of the dependent field.
   */
  dependent_field_value?: string;
  /**
   * The field whose value was received.
   */
  provided_field_name?: string;
  /**
   * The value that was received.
   */
  provided_field_value?: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingDependencyDependency {
  /**
   * The dependent field name.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The dependent field value.
   */
  field_value: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestMissingRequiredField {
  /**
   * The missing field's name.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestParseError {}
/**
 * Error indicating that the request contained one or more stale schema
 * fragments, which are schema fragments that have been replaced by a
 * newer version and are therefore considered deprecated schema fragments.
 * The caller should refresh and use the latest schema fragments in their
 * request.
 *
 */
export interface ErrorBadRequestStaleSchemaFragments {}
export interface ErrorBadRequestUnexpectedJsonType {
  actual: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  expected: "array" | "bool" | "null" | "number" | "object" | "string";
  /**
   * The field name that's invalid.
   */
  field_name: string;
}
export interface ErrorBadRequestValueNotPermitted {
  /**
   * The allowed values for the field.
   */
  allowed_values?: string[];
  /**
   * The field whose value is not permitted.
   */
  field_name: string;
  /**
   * The reason the value isn't permitted.
   */
  reason?: string;
}

```

</Accordion>
